### Round 2: Malaysian Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-04-08*

#### Qualifying ELO Changes

### Round 3: Bahrain Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-04-15*

#### Qualifying ELO Changes

| Driver | Constructor | Position | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | Result | vs Teammate |

### Round 4: Spanish Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-05-13*

### Round 10: European Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-07-22*

#### Qualifying ELO Changes

*Date: 2007-09-16*

| Driver | Constructor | Position | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | Result | vs Teammate |

### Round 17: Brazilian Grand Prix
*Date: 2007-10-21*

#### Qualifying ELO Changes

| Driver | Constructor | Position | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | Result | vs Teammate |
